module: srl_nokia-acl
  +--rw acl
     +--rw ipv4-filter* [name]
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro forwarding-complex* [complex-identifier]
     |     |     +--ro complex-identifier    string
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?      uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?          uint16
     |     |     +--ro output-total?         uint16
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw log?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2cp}?
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw dscp-set*           srl_nokia-comm:dscp
     |     |  +--rw fragment?           boolean
     |     |  +--rw first-fragment?     boolean
     |     |  +--rw icmp
     |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp-type
     |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  +--rw protocol?           srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw source-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro per-interface
     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw ipv6-filter* [name]
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro forwarding-complex* [complex-identifier]
     |     |     +--ro complex-identifier    string
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?      uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?          uint16
     |     |     +--ro output-total?         uint16
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw log?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2cp}?
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  +--rw dscp-set*           srl_nokia-comm:dscp
     |     |  +--rw icmp6
     |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp6-type
     |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  +--rw next-header?        srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw source-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro per-interface
     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw mac-filter* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:disabled}?
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro forwarding-complex* [complex-identifier]
     |     |     +--ro complex-identifier    string
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?      uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?          uint16
     |     |     +--ro output-total?         uint16
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw log?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2cp}?
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-mac
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  +--rw ethertype?         srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ethertype
     |     |  +--rw source-mac
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  +--rw vlan
     |     |     +--rw outermost-vlan-id
     |     |        +--rw (vlan-matching-type)?
     |     |           +--:(range-with-one-value)
     |     |           |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |           |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |           +--:(range-with-two-values)
     |     |           |  +--rw range
     |     |           |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |           |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |           +--:(special-value-none-to-match-untagged)
     |     |              +--rw none?       empty
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta

     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw cpm-filter
     |  +--rw ipv4-filter
     |  |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?   boolean
     |  |  +--ro last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |  |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32

     |  |     |     |     +--rw log?          boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2cp}?
     |  |     |     |     +--rw rate-limit
     |  |     |     |        +--rw system-cpu-policer?    -> ../../../../../../../policers/system-cpu-policer/name
     |  |     |     |        +--rw distributed-policer?   -> ../../../../../../../policers/policer/name {srl_nokia-feat:trident3 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-vsrl or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2cp or srl_nokia-feat:trident4 or srl_nokia-feat:monterey}?

     |  |        |  +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        |  +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

     |  |        |  +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

module: srl_nokia-routing-policy
  +--rw routing-policy!
     +--rw as-path-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name          srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw expression?   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-path-regexp
     +--rw prefix-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name      srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw prefix* [ip-prefix mask-length-range]
     |     +--rw ip-prefix            srl_nokia-comm:ip-prefix
     |     +--rw mask-length-range    string
     +--rw community-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name      srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw member*   union
     +--rw policy* [name]
        +--rw name              srl_nokia-comm:name
        +--rw default-action
        |  +--rw reject!
        |  +--rw accept!
        |  |  +--rw bgp!
        |  |     +--rw as-path!
        |  |     |  +--rw remove?    boolean
        |  |     |  +--rw replace*   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-number
        |  |     |  +--rw prepend!
        |  |     |     +--rw as-number?   union
        |  |     |     +--rw repeat-n?    uint8
        |  |     +--rw communities
        |  |     |  +--rw add?       -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |  |     |  +--rw remove?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |  |     |  +--rw replace?   -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |  |     +--rw local-preference
        |  |     |  +--rw set?   uint32
        |  |     +--rw med {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-bgp-med}?
        |  |     |  +--rw set?   union
        |  |     +--rw origin
        |  |        +--rw set?   enumeration
        |  +--rw next-entry! {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-fallthrough-actions}?
        |  +--rw next-policy! {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-fallthrough-actions}?
        +--rw statement* [sequence-id]
           +--rw sequence-id    uint32
           +--rw match!
           |  +--rw family?       srl_nokia-pol-types:bgp-family-type
           |  +--rw prefix-set?   -> /routing-policy/prefix-set/name
           |  +--rw bgp!
           |  |  +--rw as-path-set?      -> /routing-policy/as-path-set/name
           |  |  +--rw as-path-length!
           |  |  |  +--rw value       uint8
           |  |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pol-types:comparison-operator-type
           |  |  |  +--rw unique?     boolean
           |  |  +--rw community-set?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
           |  |  +--rw evpn
           |  |     +--rw route-type*   uint8
           |  +--rw protocol?     identityref
           |  +--rw isis
           |  |  +--rw level?        uint8
           |  |  +--rw route-type?   enumeration
           |  +--rw ospf
           |     +--rw area-id?       srl_nokia-ospf-types:ospf-area-identifier
           |     +--rw route-type?    identityref
           |     +--rw instance-id?   uint32
           +--rw action
              +--rw reject!
              +--rw accept!
              |  +--rw bgp!
              |     +--rw as-path!
              |     |  +--rw remove?    boolean
              |     |  +--rw replace*   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-number
              |     |  +--rw prepend!
              |     |     +--rw as-number?   union
              |     |     +--rw repeat-n?    uint8
              |     +--rw communities
              |     |  +--rw add?       -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
              |     |  +--rw remove?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
              |     |  +--rw replace?   -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
              |     +--rw local-preference
              |     |  +--rw set?   uint32
              |     +--rw med {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-bgp-med}?
              |     |  +--rw set?   union
              |     +--rw origin
              |        +--rw set?   enumeration
              +--rw next-entry! {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-fallthrough-actions}?
              +--rw next-policy! {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-fallthrough-actions}?

     +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:vxlan-tunnel
        +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:vtep* [address]
        |  +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:address        srl_nokia-comm:ip-address

        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?               srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-packets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
        +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:statistics {srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d2 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d3 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-vsrl}?
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?            srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
